Tá an ceantar seo go hálainn.
??
This region is beautiful.

Tá áiseanna maithe ann agus tá muintir na háite go deas.

??
There are nice houses here.

Dia duit. Dia is Muire duit.
??

Tá mé go breá.
??
I am fine. [in aswer to 'how are you']

Níl caill orm.
??

Go diail!
??

??

??

??

??

??

??

??

??
Carna [a place in County Galway] is nice.

Tá an solas sin briste.
??

??

??

??

Beagnach deich mbliana ó shin d'éirigh mé as an leaba in árasán beag.

??

Cuireadh cána i gceantar na Cairibe agus cadás níos faide siar agus ó thuaidh.
??
Cane was planted in the Caribbean area and cotton further west and north.

Ar ndóigh ba ag freastal ar na margaí siúcra agus éadaí ar ais san Eoraip a bhí na trádálaithe.
??
Of course, the traders were serving the sugar and clothes markets back in Europe.

Ach bhí an comórtas géar idir na soláthróirí, agus bhí na brabaigh caol.
??
But competition between the suppliers was fierce and the profits were narrow.

Ní raibh úinéirí na n-eastát in ann oibrithe a mhealladh as an Eoraip ná as Meiriceá.
??
Estate owners were not able to attract workers from Europe to America.

Thosaíodar mar sin ag ceannach oibrithe as an Afraic.
??
So, they started buying workers from Africa.

Caithfear cuimhneamh go...
??
It has to be remembered that...

As an am seo amach b'iad sclábhaithe formhór mór na ndaoine gorma a facthas san Eoraip agus sa domhan nua.
??
From this time onward, most black people seen in Europe and the new world were slaves.

Níorbh fhada gur thosaigh daoine geala ag breathnú ar dhaoine gorma mar fho-chine.
??
It wasn't long before white people started looking at black people as a sub-race.

Níorbh fhada gur thosaigh feachtais in aghaidh na sclábhaíochta.
??
It wasn't long until anti-slavery campaigns started.

Faoi dheireadh an 17ú haois bhí deireadh le húinéireacht sclábhaithe san Eoraip.
??
By the end of the 17th century slave ownership was ended in Europe.

Faoin mbliain 1776 bhí deireadh le sclábhaíocht i roinnt de na stáit thuaidh.
??
By the year 1776 slavery was ended in many of the northern states.

Mar a leath an tír siar amach, tháinig níos mó stáit isteach san aontacht nár ghlac le sclábhaíocht.
??
As the country spread out west, more states joined the union that did not accept slavery.

Cé nárbh é an sclábhaíocht an t-aon chúis le cogadh cathartha na Stát Aontaithe, ba cheist lárnach í.
??
Although slavery was not the only cause of the United States civil war, it was a central question.

Faoi 1865 bhí úinéaracht daoine in aghaidh an dlí in gach ceann de na Stáit Aontaithe.
??
By 1865, owning people was against the law in each of the United States.

Ní raibh cearta iomlána ag daoine Gorma.
??
Black people did not have full rights.

In 1856 rialaigh Cúirt Uachtarach na Stát Aontaithe nár bhain bille cearta na tíre le daoine Gorma.
??
In 1856 the United States Supreme Court ruled that the country's bill of rights did not apply to Black people.

Bhí an capall ag tochas a chos ar an urlár.

The horse was scratching his foot on the floor.

Bí siúráilte greim sceadamáin a bhreith orthu agus a dtachtadh.
??
Make sure to grab them by the throat and strangle them.

Ní ligfeadh an eagla do Shéimí cur suas don obair.
??
Fear didn't allow Jamie to refuse doing it.

Ní raibh rún ar bith gadaíochta aige.
??
He didn't really want to steal.

Beidh a fhios agat gan greim eiteoga a fháil ar chirc.
??
You will know you shouldn't grab a hen by its wing.

Bhail, sin an seachtú haithne agat, is déan a mhór nó a bheag di.
??
Well, that's the seventh commandment for you, whatever you think of it.

Níor chuala mé gadaíocht curtha síos dó riamh.
??
I've never heard him being accused of stealing.

Is cuma duit ar an tsaol seo ach goid de réir dlí.
??
All you need to care aboit in this world is to steal in a way the law allows.

Is furast duitse stad den ól nuair nár thúsaigh tú air.
??
It's easy for you to stop drinking when you haven't started.

Ba doilig bheith ina gcuideachta gan a bheith mar dhuine acu féin.
??
It was difficult to be in with them without turning into one of them.

An bhfuil do sháith agat?
??
Have you got enough? {after beating}

'Bhfuil a fhios agat goidé mo chomhairlese duit?
??
You know what my advice to you is?

Ná blais aon deor den bheoir mhallaithe le do lá.
??
Don't taste a single drop of that damned beer as long as you live.

Is cuma dá mbíodh siad ag magadh ort go dtiteadh an cár astu.
??
It doesn't matter if they mock you until their teeth fall out.

Mo chreach agus mo chrá gan mé chomh hóg leatsa inniu. Chaithfinn saol nár chaith mé.
??
If only I was as young as you today. I'd spend my live differently.

Ba róbheag a shamhail mé go n-imeoinn mar a d'imigh mé.
??
I hardly imagined I'd leave the way I did.

Ní raibh acu ach mé.
??
I was their only child.

Thug siad scoil agus léann domh ar feadh a n-acmhainne.
??
They gave me as much education as they could afford.

Is maith is cuimhin liom an tráthnóna a d'imigh mé.
??
I remember well the afternoon I left.

Ba é sin an t-amharc deireanach a fuair mé orthu.
??
That was the last I saw of them.

Níl léamh nó scríobh nó inse béil ar an ghrá a thug mise don chailín udaí.
??
There is no describing the love I had for that girl.

Ná bím ag caoineadh! Bíodh foighid agam!
??
Don't cry! Be patient! {to self}

Ní raibh eagla le cur orm.
??
Nothing could scare me.

Síleann tú an cineál seo cainte a bheith iontach ag mo leithéidse.
??
You think it's strange for me to talk like that.

Bhí mise ar feadh míosa ar mo sheachnadh.
??
I was in hiding for a month.

Thóg siad ó mo leaba mé uair roimh an lá.
??
They took me out of my bed an hour before daybreak.

An lá fuair mé cead na coise b'éadrom mo chroí.
??
The day I was set free I felt happy.

Chuaigh mé in éadóchas.
??
I became desparate.

Nuair a bheadh an saol fá chónaí...
??
When everybody was asleep...

Goidé tháinig uirthi?
??
What happened to her?

Bhí fuath na námhad agam air i mo chroí.
??
I hated him passionately with all my heart.

D'ól mé agus d'ól mé gur chaill mé mo mheabhair agus mo stuaim.
??
I drank and I drank until I lost my sense and my good judgment.

Tá mé thar chomhairle anois.
??
I am beyond advice now.

Ná thabhair grá do chroí choíche do mhnaoi.
??
Don't ever fall in love with a woman.

Thug 'ach aon duine acu lámh is focal don duine eile.
??
They all made a promise to one another.

Solais loinnireacha gheala a bhainfeadh an t-amharc as an tsúil agat.
??
Bright shining lights that would blinden you.

Sheasaigh Séimí agus a thaca le coirnéal.
??
Jamie stood leaning against a corner.

Cá háit a leagfaidh mé mo cheann go maidin?
??
Where will I rest my head tonight?

Bhí na sráideanna ag bánú agus na solais ag gabháil as.
??
The streets we emptying and the lights were going out.

Chaill sé a mheabhair glan.
??
He lost his mind completely.

Dar leis gur cheart dó glór a chinn a aithne.
??
He thought he should recognize his voice.

Lá arna mhárach bhí Séimí arís ina chruth féin.
??
The next morning Jamie was his old self again.

Bhain sé slogóg eile as.
??
He drank another gulp from it.

D'ól 'ach aon fhear acu tarraingt a chinn den bhuidéal.
??
Each man drank his fill from the bottle.

Bhí truaigh an tsaoil aige do Mhicheál Dubh agus don bhail a chuir an bhantracht air.
??
He felt sorry for Micheál Dubh and for what women did to him.

B'éigean dó luí ar phutóga folmha go maidin.
??
He would have to go to sleep on an empty stomach.

Ní thiocfadh leis a ghabháil chun an bhaile ar phócaí folmha.
??
He could not come home with empty pockets.

Nach raibh go leor den fhear ann?
??
Wasn't he man enough?

Ní dhéanfadh sé a dhath choíche a ghoinfeadh a croí.
??
He would never do anything to hurt her.

Bhí coiscéim throm leis.
??
He was walking heavily.

Bhí sé ag spágáil leis fríd an tsneachta.
??
He was wading through the snow.

Tamall beag i ndiaidh a ghabháil ó sholas dó...
??
A little while after it got dark...

Bhí siad fá shiúl lae don áit.
??
They were a day's walk from the place.

Bhí a phócaí ag brúchtaigh leis an ór.
??
His pockets were bursting with gold.

Bheadh sé uilig thart anois agus bheinn as buaireamh.
??
It would all be over now and my troubles would be no more.

Is aige atá ábhar na ndeor.
??
He has something to cry about.

Bhí an baile mór fá chupla céad míle dóibh.
??
The city was a couple hundred miles away.

Tógadh sa doras ag a chéile iad.
??
They grew up next door to each other.

D'éist sí. Ní raibh ní ba mhó le mothachtáil.
??
She listened. Nothing more could be heard.

Dar le Babaí gurbh é a ceart an glór cinn sin a aithne, ach ní raibh dul aici smaoineamh cá háit a gcuala sí é.
??
Babaí thought she should recognize that voice but couldn't remember where she had heard it.

Bhí lúcháir mhór ar Bhabaí roimhe.
??
Babaí was very happy to see him. {to welcome him when he arrived}

Cá raibh sé le fada riamh?
??
Where was he all that time?

Thost sé.
??
He paused {speaking}.

Ansin smaoinigh sé nach raibh sin inráite aige.
??
Then he realized he shouldn't have said that.

Tháinig na deora leis.
??
Tears came into his eyes.

Is minic a chuala mé m'athair ag scéalaíocht ort.
??
I often heard my father talking about you.

Bhí cos amuigh is cos istigh san uaigh aige.
??
He was one foot in the grave.

Ar béal maidine.
??
First thing in the morning.

Ní raibh as a mbéal ach an cogadh.
??
All they talked about was the war.

Is mór an gar gan an duine bocht a bheith istigh.
??
It's a good thing the poor man isn't in.

Tá na gunnaí aimsithe ar an doras acu.
??
They have their guns pointed at the door.

Níl sé inleighis.
??
He cannot be cured.

An bhfuil sé inleighis, a shagairt?
??
Can he be cured, father?

Níl gar a bheith ag caint.
??
There's no point saying anything.

Nocht an tEargal.
??
Errigal appeared {emerged from behind the horizon}.

Bhí sé ag gabháil ó sholas de.
??
It was getting dark.

Bhí truaigh aige dóibh, ach truaigh gan tarrtháil a bhí inti.
??
He felt sorry for them but there was nothing he could do for them.

Níl feidhm orm aon lá oibre a dhéanamh le mo sholas. Tá mé i mo sháith den tsaol.
??
I don't have to work a single day for as long as I live. I am rich.

Plátaí airgid a bhainfeadh an t-amharc as an tsúil agat.
??
Plates of gold that would make you blind.

Ní raibh dul ag aon duine a aithne.
??
Nobody could recognize him.

Ba é sin mo ghnóithe an bealach.
??
That's why I came here.
